< review>
After a very minor accident, my wife brought her car to this shop based on Geico's recommendation and it's proximity to our home... And I'm so glad we did!

Crazy efficient process. Geico claims guy was there, rental car was there, shop manager inspected the car in no time. We we're off in a new set of wheels in around 15 minutes.

Repair time was about a week, which we did get slightly impatient about but quality work takes time... And yes, it was worth it.

Picking up the car was as seamless as dropping it off. Bill had already been covered by insurance, rental car went back to it's home, and we were on our way. Upon closer inspection the car was better than it was prior to the accident. Had a couple spots polished that weren't part of the damage, they replaced a headlight free of charge, and whatever they used to clean the plastic trim on the car makes this thing look like a million bucks

After this experience, I'd recommend anyone to get into a fender bender just so they have a good excuse to visit this shop. I'm kidding, don't wreck your car on purpose... But if you want to freshen up a car then visit some of the friendliest automotive folks in town at Chilton<//review>
